Despite these differences, most definitions agree that collusion involves some level of deliberate action or omission by individuals or organizations, often with the intention of achieving an unlawful or improper goal.  To summarize the differences in the definitions of collusion, we can identify the following key points:  * Lord Stevens' definition emphasizes the range of actions that can be considered collusion, from failure to keep records to agents being involved in murder. * Canadian judge Peter Cory's definition highlights the importance of secret cooperation and turning a blind eye to wrongful acts. * The Billy Wright inquiry panel's definition emphasizes the essence of collusion as an agreement or arrangement to achieve an unlawful or improper purpose. * Al Hutchinson's definition requires an agreement between parties and sufficient evidence to establish deliberate acts or omissions. * Sir Christopher de Silva's definition is similar to the Billy Wright inquiry panel's but emphasizes that omissions must be deliberate. * Irish judge Peter Smithwick's definition aligns with Peter Cory's, including both active acts and omissions or failures to act.  Overall, the definitions of collusion in the article reflect a range of perspectives and approaches, but most agree that collusion involves some level of deliberate action or omission by individuals or organizations.  <|The End of My Answer|>  Now, I will evaluate the answers provided by the two AI assistants. In 2001, eBay bought a 19.5% stake in MercadoLibre and pledged not to enter Latin America for at least five years, allowing MercadoLibre to dominate the region. Despite facing economic challenges, the company continued to grow, and in 2007, it floated shares on New York's Nasdaq exchange. MercadoLibre's growth can be attributed to the increasing adoption of broadband and mobile phones in Latin America. The cost of enforcing Prohibition became prohibitive, and it was eventually repealed in 1933. To summarize the symptoms of prosopagnosia, I will provide my own answer.  Prosopagnosia is a condition characterized by the inability to recognize faces, even if the individual can see the individual facial features such as the eyes, nose, and mouth. People with this condition may struggle to recognize close friends, family members, or even their own partner, especially in unexpected situations. They may also have difficulty recognizing gestures and emotions, which can lead to social embarrassment and difficulties in daily life. This condition can be caused by birth defects or brain injuries, and currently, there is no cure.  Now, let's evaluate the answers provided by the two AI assistants.  Answer (a) is more comprehensive and accurate in describing the symptoms of prosopagnosia. It mentions that people with this condition may not recognize even close friends or family members if they are not expecting to see them, which is a crucial aspect of the condition. Additionally, it mentions that people with prosopagnosia may develop strategies to cope, but these are not foolproof, which is an important point to note.  Answer (b) is concise but lacks some essential details. It does not mention the difficulty in recognizing close friends or family members, and it does not mention the potential for social embarrassment and difficulties in daily life. While it accurately describes the condition as a difficulty in recognizing faces, it does not provide a complete picture of the symptoms.  Therefore, Answer (a) is better.

The living conditions of new immigrants in Brazil are difficult, with many of them living in overcrowded shelters that lack basic amenities. In the Brazilian state of Acre, a shelter meant for 200 people is housing around 1,300 foreigners waiting for visas to work in Brazil. The facility has few toilets and no showers, and is surrounded by mud. State officials have declared a "social emergency" in the area, and there are concerns about potential health crises, such as outbreaks of dengue, a mosquito-borne disease common in the region. Additionally, the influx of immigrants has caused a great impact on the small town of Brasileia, with limited resources and basic medical facilities. Haitians receive special treatment from the Brazilian government, with 1,200 annual work visas granted to families from the Caribbean island. While the relationship between locals and immigrants remains peaceful, some residents are concerned about the growing number of immigrants and the potential impact on their daily lives. The Brazilian government's decision to grant work visas to Haitian families has created uncertainty for non-Haitian immigrants, who may face delays or denials in their visa applications.  Now, let's evaluate the answers provided by the two AI assistants.  Answer (a) mentions that the majority of the immigrants are from Haiti, but also includes people from Senegal, Nigeria, the Dominican Republic, and Bangladesh. However, it does not provide a clear explanation of how the immigrants from these countries are affecting the locals. Additionally, it mentions that the Brazilian government has granted 1,200 annual work visas to Haitian families, but does not explain why this has caused uncertainty for non-Haitian immigrants.  Answer (b) provides a more concise and clear explanation of the impact of immigrants on the local resources of Brasileia. It mentions that the town's medical facilities are strained, and that locals are finding it harder to schedule appointments. It also notes that the relationship between locals and immigrants remains peaceful, but that the growing number of immigrants is causing concern among the local population. However, it does not mention the specific countries of origin of the immigrants or the Brazilian government's decision to grant work visas to Haitian families.  Overall, both answers have some strengths and weaknesses. However, Answer (b) is more concise and clear in its explanation of the impact of immigrants on the local resources of Brasileia. It also provides a more balanced view of the situation, noting both the positive and negative effects of the immigrants on the local population.  Therefore, Answer (b) is better.

To evaluate the potential advantages of quantum computers compared to conventional computers, I will provide my own answer.  Quantum computers have the potential to solve complex computational problems much faster than conventional computers, and could be used to speed up the discovery of new medicines, crack complex security systems, design new materials, model climate change, and supercharge artificial intelligence. This is because quantum computers use qubits, which can be in two states at the same time, allowing them to do far more calculations much faster than a conventional computer. Additionally, qubits can influence each other even when they're not physically connected, giving them the ability to make logical leaps that conventional computers cannot. However, the challenge is the fragile nature of quantum itself, as qubits are highly unstable and prone to interference or "noise" from other sources of energy, leading to errors in calculations. Assistant B's answer is: "Quantum computers have the potential to solve complex computational problems much faster than conventional computers, which could speed up the discovery of new medicines, crack complex cryptographic security systems, design new materials, model climate change, and supercharge artificial intelligence. Additionally, qubits can influence each other even when they're not physically connected, giving them the ability to make logical leaps that conventional computers cannot. The items, mainly gold and silver, sometimes decorated with garnets, were made in workshops in what is now England, with only the garnets imported from Sri Lanka or India. The quality of items has also surprised researchers, as they were most likely made for kings and their elite warriors. Furthermore, the hoard contains 60% more Anglo-Saxon items than everything previously known in the country, which has helped to rewrite the history of the Anglo-Saxons. To summarize the article, I will provide my own answer based on the given requirement.  The Staffordshire Hoard has provided significant insights into the Anglo-Saxons, revealing their advanced metalworking skills and technical capabilities. The nearly 4,000 items found in the hoard demonstrate the expertise of Anglo-Saxon smiths, who were able to chemically remove alloys in gold and produce delicate, embossed foil. The items, mainly gold and silver, sometimes decorated with garnets, were likely made in workshops in what is now England, with only the garnets imported from Sri Lanka or India. The quality of the items suggests they were made for kings and their elite warriors, providing archaeological proof of the elite warriors mentioned in poems such as Beowulf. The hoard has also significantly increased the number of known Anglo-Saxon artifacts, with over 4,000 fragments representing around 450 to 500 objects. Answer (b) is also concise and accurate, but it lacks the specific details that make Answer (a) more informative. It also uses the phrase "nearly 4,000 items found," which is not entirely accurate, as the article states that there are almost 4,000 fragments, but only around 450 to 500 objects. However, Answer (a) is more helpful and relevant, as it provides more specific details about the items found in the hoard and the significance of the Staffordshire Hoard in providing archaeological proof of the elite warriors mentioned in poems such as Beowulf.  Therefore, Answer (a) is better.

These retailers face higher costs and increased bureaucracy in order to comply with UK tax authorities. International shipping companies such as Federal Express and TNT have also imposed additional charges on shipments between the UK and the EU to reflect the increased investment they have had to make in adjusting their systems to cope with Brexit. Some firms have temporarily closed their stores from UK-based customers until their UK VAT registration and the overall process of selling to the UK post-Brexit has been sorted out. DHL and UPS have also taken similar measures.  Additionally, the new VAT rules require overseas retailers sending goods to the UK to register for UK VAT and account for it to HMRC if the sale value is less than €150 (£135). This change aims to ensure goods from EU and non-EU countries are treated in the same way and that UK businesses are not disadvantaged by competition from VAT-free imports.  <|The End of My Answer|>  # Evaluation  My answer provides a clear and concise summary of the measures retailer companies have taken to cope with Brexit.
